if (is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js') && (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js') != '8b37a9f8b2f3c1134907fcf29b52e8340a7d8340')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js') != '8b37a9f8b2f3c1134907fcf29b52e8340a7d8340') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/setup.js');
}

if (is_file('setup/setup_base.js') && (sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') != '1bc1d090cf90d850005906e8a2accfe1f4f289f8')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup_base.js');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup_base.js');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_9();
if (!is_file('setup/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup_base.js');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') != '1bc1d090cf90d850005906e8a2accfe1f4f289f8') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup_base.js');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup_base.js');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'eee96e3a5b3cf81af384fcc77cc4b5faa76bcc37') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'eee96e3a5b3cf81af384fcc77cc4b5faa76bcc37') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '522d8db16f40627b725d0c9ac90b30e4b1c46671') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'eee96e3a5b3cf81af384fcc77cc4b5faa76bcc37') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '2d9183009a768c6a70cf16ca49d6fb6d93089ab1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '59547035d621c6c8bf5401101c2c263b13aafe68') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') != '71c5793ab52250c19447f1476605ce7e07f65aa8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '71c5793ab52250c19447f1476605ce7e07f65aa8') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '160f54086674f64e9b8f898178a6b11b1cb73c12') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '71c5793ab52250c19447f1476605ce7e07f65aa8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_27();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'cf230c7ed620334c2a5d9709fc83a9b755528759') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'cf230c7ed620334c2a5d9709fc83a9b755528759') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '65bab888323f52b94842329c10dfb9d502990329') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'cf230c7ed620334c2a5d9709fc83a9b755528759') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_32();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != 'ca250da7720163e713a43c46f39f6027bb767e9a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'ca250da7720163e713a43c46f39f6027bb767e9a') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '8a5fa390ef4d231620535ac657eca8ec5e1ad41e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_32();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'ca250da7720163e713a43c46f39f6027bb767e9a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}
